### `ByteTag_vtbl`
```
struct /*VFT*/ ByteTag_vtbl
{
  void (__fastcall *~Tag)(Tag *this);
  void (__fastcall *deleteChildren)(Tag *this);
  void (__fastcall *write)(Tag *this, IDataOutput *);
  void (__fastcall *load)(Tag *this, IDataInput *);
```
